\DoxyCodeLine{00429                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} total\_seconds == 0:}

\DoxyCodeLine{00431                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00432                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} total\_seconds < 0:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00433                                 \_svalue += \textcolor{stringliteral}{'-\/'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00434                                 total\_seconds *= -\/1}

\DoxyCodeLine{00437                             hours = total\_seconds // 3600}
\DoxyCodeLine{00438                             minutes = (total\_seconds -\/ (hours * 3600)) // 60}
\DoxyCodeLine{00439                             \_svalue += \textcolor{stringliteral}{'\{0:02d\}:\{1:02d\}'}.format(}
\DoxyCodeLine{00440                                 hours, minutes)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00441             \textcolor{keywordflow}{except} AttributeError:}

\DoxyCodeLine{00426                     tzoff = input\_data.tzinfo.utcoffset(input\_data)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00427                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} tzoff \textcolor{keywordflow}{is} \textcolor{keywordflow}{not} \textcolor{keywordtype}{None}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00428                         total\_seconds = tzoff.seconds + (86400 * tzoff.days)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00429                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} total\_seconds == 0:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00430                             \_svalue += \textcolor{stringliteral}{'Z'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00431                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00432                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} total\_seconds < 0:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00433                                 \_svalue += \textcolor{stringliteral}{'-\/'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00434                                 total\_seconds *= -\/1}
\DoxyCodeLine{00435                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00436                                 \_svalue += \textcolor{stringliteral}{'+'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00437                             hours = total\_seconds // 3600}
\DoxyCodeLine{00438                             minutes = (total\_seconds -\/ (hours * 3600)) // 60}
\DoxyCodeLine{00439                             \_svalue += \textcolor{stringliteral}{'\{0:02d\}:\{1:02d\}'}.format(}
\DoxyCodeLine{00440                                 hours, minutes)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00441             \textcolor{keywordflow}{except} AttributeError:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00442                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{pass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00443             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \_svalue}
